[2;36m                    [0m           • The code path continues through `TextExtractor.processGroupEnd` and             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `RTFParser.parse`. The fuzzer harness calls `RTFParser.parseInline` → `parse` →     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `parseOne` → `fuzzerTestOneInput`.                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • No filtering or validation of the serialized form is evident in the RTF parser  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         components, allowing arbitrary payloads to reach the deserialization API.           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Areas for investigation                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           To obtain a comprehensive view of the issue, review:                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m1[0m. RTFEmbObjHandler.handleCompletedObject and its use of `ObjectInputStream` for  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         embedded object deserialization.                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m2[0m. TextExtractor and RTFParser code paths that lead to `[1;35mreadObject[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` invocation. [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m3[0m. Any custom implementations of `readObject` or `readResolve` in classes on the  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         classpath that could be abused.                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m4[0m. The Jazzer harness wrapper [1m([0m`jaz.Zer.readObject` and                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `jaz.Zer.reportFindingIfEnabled`[1m)[0m to understand how findings are detected and       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         reported.                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Note: The fuzzer harness itself is only the entry point and does not represent the  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         root cause. The core issue lies in unguarded deserialization logic within the RTF   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         handling code.                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         A Jazzer fuzzing run against Apache Tika’s RTF parser [1m([0mRTFEmbObjHandler[1m)[0m reported a [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         high-severity finding: unbounded Java object deserialization in the                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         EMB_STATE.JAVA_OBJDATA branch, risking remote code execution. A patch was           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         introduced that skips unsafe deserialization, records only metadata, and calls      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35mreset[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` to terminate processing. After applying the patch, compilation failed due [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         to an undefined symbol `TikaCoreProperties.CONTENT_TYPE_OVERRIDE`.                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m. Initial Issue                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - A fuzzer [1m([0mJazzer[1m)[0m triggered `FuzzerSecurityIssueHigh: Remote Code Execution`   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         during RTF parsing.                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Stack trace pinpoints `[1;35mRTFEmbObjHandler.readObject[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m` invoking `new         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mObjectInputStream[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m[1;35m.readObject[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`.                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - External data controls the class name, allowing instantiation of arbitrary     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         classes on the classpath.                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m. Key Observations from the Issue                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Unsafe use of Java deserialization within the RTF embed handler.               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - No validation or class filtering prior to streaming bytes into                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `ObjectInputStream`.                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Metadata is set based on the deserialized object's class name and content,     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         then passed to `extractObj`.                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m. Patch Attempt                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The EMB_STATE.JAVA_OBJDATA branch was replaced with logic to:                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Skip deserialization entirely.                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Set `RTFMetadata.EMB_CLASS` to “deserialization-skipped”.                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Override content type via `TikaCoreProperties.CONTENT_TYPE_OVERRIDE`.        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Record raw data length in `Metadata.CONTENT_LENGTH`.                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Invoke `[1;35mreset[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` and return immediately.                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Original lines [1;36m212[0m–[1;36m230[0m were removed and replaced as shown in the patch.        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m. Patch Result and Compilation Log                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Maven compilation error in `RTFEmbObjHandler.java` at the line setting         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `CONTENT_TYPE_OVERRIDE`.                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Error message:                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         org.apache.tika.metadata.TikaCoreProperties”                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - All other modules compiled successfully; only the Microsoft parser module      [2m                [0m
